A massive, ancient temple-like complex with these key features:

Main structure built primarily of stone bricks and smooth stone
Central courtyard surrounded by tall, imposing walls
Four corner towers, each approximately 40 blocks tall and 10 blocks in diameter
Walls connecting the towers, about 30 blocks tall and 5 blocks thick
Stepped pyramid structure in the center, rising to about 25 blocks high
Grand staircase leading up to the pyramid, approximately 15 blocks wide
Small pond or water feature at the base of the stairs
Intricate pathways made of stone slabs connecting different areas
Multiple levels and platforms throughout the complex
Small structures or shrines on top of the walls
Decorative elements using stairs and slabs to create depth and detail
Large arched entrance in the front wall, about 5 blocks wide and 7 blocks tall

Provide step-by-step instructions on how to construct this elaborate temple complex, including:

Exact dimensions for the overall structure, walls, towers, and central pyramid
Block types to use for different sections (e.g., stone bricks, smooth stone, slabs)
Detailed instructions for building the corner towers, including any decorative elements
How to construct the central stepped pyramid and its grand staircase
Placement and design of pathways, including the main path leading to the entrance
Instructions for creating the water feature and surrounding landscape within the complex
Details on how to build the arched entrance and any other openings in the walls
Guidance on adding decorative elements and small structures on top of the walls
Tips for ensuring symmetry and balance in the overall design

Ensure the description captures the monumental scale and ancient, weathered appearance of the structure. Include suggestions for creating an aged look using a mix of similar block types and strategic placement of stairs and slabs.
